about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2> <p>This lecture provided
  an overview on artificial intelligence and took a deep dive on machine learning,
  including supervised learning, unsupervised learning, and reinforcement learning.</p>
  <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Jeremy Kepner, Vijay Gadepally</p>

  <span m="198189">is</span> <span m="198583">the</span> <span m="198978">theory</span>

  <span m="200555">computer</span> <span m="200950">systems</span> <span m="201382">that</span>
  <span m="201814">perform</span> <span m="202246">tasks</span> <span m="202679">that</span>
  <span m="203111">augment</span> <span m="203543">for</span> <span m="203976">human</span>
  <span m="204408">intelligence,</span> <span m="204840">such</span> <span m="205273">as</span>
  <span m="205705">perceiving,</span> <span m="206137">classifying,</span> <span m="206570">learning,</span>
  <span m="207266">abstracting,</span> <span m="207962">reasoning,</span> <span m="208658">and/or</span>

  <span m="1070641">can</span> <span m="1070999">be</span> <span m="1071357">very,</span>
  <span m="1071714">very</span> <span m="1072072">valuable</span> <span m="1072430">to</span>
  <span m="1072788">your</span> <span m="1073146">work</span> <span m="1073504">and</span>
  <span m="1073861">the</span> <span m="1074219">work</span> <span m="1074577">of</span>
  <span m="1074935">many</span> <span m="1075293">other</span> <span m="1075651">people.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1077703">back</span> <span m="1078017">to</span> <span m="1078331">the</span>
  <span m="1078645">AI</span> <span m="1078959">architecture,</span> <span m="1079273">we're</span>
  <span m="1079587">going</span> <span m="1079901">to</span> <span m="1080215">just</span>
  <span m="1080529">go</span> <span m="1080843">through</span> <span m="1081157">very</span>

  <span m="1084501">piece</span> <span m="1084845">we're</span> <span m="1085188">going</span>
  <span m="1085531">to</span> <span m="1085874">talk</span> <span m="1086217">about</span>
  <span m="1086560">is</span> <span m="1086903">data</span> <span m="1087246">conditioning,</span>
  <span m="1087590">which</span> <span m="1088090">is</span> <span m="1088591">converting</span>
  <span m="1089092">unstructured</span> <span m="1089593">and</span> <span m="1090094">structured</span>
  <span m="1090595">data.</span> <span m="1091095">Within</span> <span m="1091596">the</span>
  <span m="1092097">structured</span> <span m="1092598">and</span> <span m="1093099">unstructured</span>
  <span m="1093600">data,</span> <span m="1094011">you</span> <span m="1094423">might</span>
  <span m="1094835">have</span> <span m="1095247">structured</span> <span m="1095659">sources</span>
  <span m="1096071">coming</span> <span m="1096483">from</span> <span m="1096895">sensors,</span>

  <span m="1098543">some</span> <span m="1098955">of</span> <span m="1099367">you,</span>

  <span m="2591985">the</span> <span m="2592345">world</span> <span m="2592704">of</span>
  <span m="2593063">supervised</span> <span m="2593423">learning,</span> <span m="2593782">that</span>
  <span m="2594142">could</span> <span m="2594501">be</span> <span m="2594861">the</span>
  <span m="2595220">example</span> <span m="2595580">data.</span> <span m="2595921">Or</span>
  <span m="2596263">past</span> <span m="2596605">experience</span> <span m="2596947">could</span>
  <span m="2597288">be</span> <span m="2597630">the</span> <span m="2597972">correct</span>
  <span m="2598314">label,</span> <span m="2598655">given</span> <span m="2598997">an</span>
  <span m="2599339">input</span> <span m="2599681">data</span> <span m="2600022">set</span>
  <span m="2600364">or</span> <span m="2600706">input</span> <span m="2601048">data</span>
  <span m="2601390">point.</span></p><p><span m="2603630">Machine</span> <span m="2603984">learning</span>
  <span m="2604339">is</span> <span m="2604693">a</span> <span m="2605048">combination</span>
  <span m="2605403">of</span> <span m="2605757">techniques</span> <span m="2606112">from</span>
  <span m="2606466">statistics,</span> <span m="2606821">computer,</span> <span m="2607176">and</span>
  <span m="2607530">computer</span> <span m="2607885">science</span> <span m="2608240">communities.</span>
  <span m="2608694">And</span> <span m="2609149">it's</span> <span m="2609603">the</span>
  <span m="2610058">idea</span> <span m="2610513">of</span> <span m="2610967">getting</span>
  <span m="2611422">computers</span> <span m="2611876">to</span> <span m="2612331">program</span>
  <span m="2612786">themselves.</span> <span m="2613240">Common</span> <span m="2613695">tasks</span>
  <span m="2614150">within</span> <span m="2614466">the</span> <span m="2614783">world</span>
  <span m="2615100">of</span> <span m="2615416">machine</span> <span m="2615733">learning</span>
  <span m="2616050">could</span> <span m="2616366">be</span> <span m="2616683">things</span>
  <span m="2617000">like</span> <span m="2617316">classification,</span> <span m="2617633">regression,</span>
  <span m="2617950">prediction,</span> <span m="2618765">clustering,</span> <span
  m="2619580">et</span> <span m="2620395">cetera.</span></p><p><span m="2621210">For</span>
  <span m="2621559">those</span> <span m="2621909">who</span> <span m="2622259">are</span>
  <span m="2622609">maybe</span> <span m="2622959">making</span> <span m="2623309">the</span>
  <span m="2623659">shift</span> <span m="2624009">to</span> <span m="2624359">machine</span>
  <span m="2624709">learning</span> <span m="2625059">from</span> <span m="2625409">traditional</span>
  <span m="2625759">programming,</span> <span m="2626109">I</span> <span m="2626450">found</span>
  <span m="2626792">this,</span> <span m="2627134">again,</span> <span m="2627475">from</span>
  <span m="2627817">Pedro</span> <span m="2628159">Domingos</span> <span m="2628501">to</span>
  <span m="2628842">be</span> <span m="2629184">a</span> <span m="2629526">very</span>
  <span m="2629867">useful</span> <span m="2630209">way</span> <span m="2630551">of</span>
  <span m="2630893">describing</span> <span m="2631234">it</span> <span m="2631576">to</span>
  <span m="2631918">people.</span></p><p><span m="2632260">So</span> <span m="2632529">in</span>
  <span m="2632799">traditional</span> <span m="2633069">programming,</span> <span
  m="2633339">you</span> <span m="2633609">have</span> <span m="2633879">a</span>
  <span m="2634149">data</span> <span m="2634419">set.</span> <span m="2634689">You</span>
  <span m="2634959">write</span> <span m="2635229">a</span> <span m="2635499">program,</span>
  <span m="2635769">which</span> <span m="2636039">would</span> <span m="2636309">be</span>
  <span m="2636605">if</span> <span m="2636902">you</span> <span m="2637199">see</span>
  <span m="2637495">this,</span> <span m="2637792">do</span> <span m="2638089">that.</span>
  <span m="2638386">When</span> <span m="2638682">you</span> <span m="2638979">see</span>
  <span m="2639276">this,</span> <span m="2639572">do</span> <span m="2639869">that.</span>
  <span m="2640166">For</span> <span m="2640463">this</span> <span m="2640759">many</span>
  <span m="2641056">instances,</span> <span m="2641353">do</span> <span m="2641650">the</span>
  <span m="2641885">following</span> <span m="2642121">thing</span> <span m="2642357">on</span>
  <span m="2642593">it</span> <span m="2642829">and</span> <span m="2643065">then</span>
  <span m="2643300">write</span> <span m="2643536">an</span> <span m="2643772">output</span>
  <span m="2644008">out,</span> <span m="2644244">right?</span></p><p><span m="2644480">So</span>
  <span m="2644777">you</span> <span m="2645074">input</span> <span m="2645371">a</span>
  <span m="2645668">data</span> <span m="2645965">into</span> <span m="2646262">the</span>
  <span m="2646559">program</span> <span m="2646856">into</span> <span m="2647153">a</span>
  <span m="2647450">computer,</span> <span m="2647747">and</span> <span m="2648044">the</span>
  <span m="2648341">computer</span> <span m="2648638">produces</span> <span m="2648935">an</span>
  <span m="2649232">output</span> <span m="2649530">where</span> <span m="2649842">it</span>
  <span m="2650155">says,</span> <span m="2650468">OK,</span> <span m="2650781">I've</span>
  <span m="2651094">applied</span> <span m="2651407">this</span> <span m="2651720">program</span>
  <span m="2652033">on</span> <span m="2652345">that</span> <span m="2652658">data.</span>
  <span m="2652971">And</span> <span m="2653284">this</span> <span m="2653597">gives</span>
  <span m="2653910">me</span> <span m="2654223">the</span> <span m="2654536">output.</span></p><p><span
  m="2654849">Machine</span> <span m="2655126">learning</span> <span m="2655404">is</span>
  <span m="2655681">a</span> <span m="2655959">very</span> <span m="2656236">different</span>
  <span m="2656514">way</span> <span m="2656791">of</span> <span m="2657069">thinking</span>
  <span m="2657346">about</span> <span m="2657624">it</span> <span m="2657901">in</span>
  <span m="2658179">which</span> <span m="2658456">you're</span> <span m="2658734">almost</span>
  <span m="2659011">inputting</span> <span m="2659289">the</span> <span m="2659574">data</span>
  <span m="2659860">as</span> <span m="2660146">well</span> <span m="2660431">as</span>
  <span m="2660717">the</span> <span m="2661003">output.</span></p><p><span m="2661289">So</span>
  <span m="2661554">in</span> <span m="2661820">this</span> <span m="2662086">case,</span>
  <span m="2662352">the</span> <span m="2662618">data</span> <span m="2662884">could</span>
  <span m="2663150">be</span> <span m="2663416">unlabeled</span> <span m="2663682">images.</span>
  <span m="2663948">The</span> <span m="2664214">output</span> <span m="2664480">could</span>
  <span m="2664746">be</span> <span m="2665012">the</span> <span m="2665278">labels</span>
  <span m="2665544">associated</span> <span m="2665810">with</span> <span m="2666124">those</span>
  <span m="2666438">images.</span> <span m="2666752">And</span> <span m="2667067">you</span>
  <span m="2667381">tell</span> <span m="2667695">the</span> <span m="2668010">computer,</span>
  <span m="2668324">figure</span> <span m="2668638">out</span> <span m="2668953">what</span>
  <span m="2669267">the</span> <span m="2669581">program</span> <span m="2669896">would</span>
  <span m="2670210">look</span> <span m="2670524">like.</span></p><p><span m="2670839">And</span>
  <span m="2671107">this</span> <span m="2671376">is</span> <span m="2671644">a</span>
  <span m="2671913">slightly</span> <span m="2672181">different</span> <span m="2672450">way</span>
  <span m="2672719">of</span> <span m="2672987">thinking</span> <span m="2673256">about</span>
  <span m="2673524">machine</span> <span m="2673793">learning</span> <span m="2674061">versus</span>
  <span m="2674330">traditional</span> <span m="2674599">programming.</span></p><p><span
  m="2676019">What</span> <span m="2676356">are</span> <span m="2676694">some</span>
  <span m="2677031">of</span> <span m="2677369">these</span> <span m="2677707">programs</span>
  <span m="2678044">or</span> <span m="2678382">algorithms</span> <span m="2678720">that</span>
  <span m="2679057">the</span> <span m="2679395">computer</span> <span m="2679733">might</span>
  <span m="2680070">use</span> <span m="2680408">to</span> <span m="2680746">figure</span>
  <span m="2681083">it</span> <span m="2681421">out?</span></p><p><span m="2681759">So</span>
  <span m="2682204">within</span> <span m="2682649">the</span> <span m="2683095">large</span>
  <span m="2683540">realm</span> <span m="2683985">of</span> <span m="2684431">machine</span>
  <span m="2684876">learning,</span> <span m="2685322">we</span> <span m="2685767">have</span>
  <span m="2686212">supervised,</span> <span m="2686658">unsupervised</span> <span

  <span m="2688279">we</span> <span m="2688645">have</span> <span m="2689010">in</span>
  <span m="2689376">the</span> <span m="2689741">brackets</span> <span m="2690106">is</span>
  <span m="2690472">essentially</span> <span m="2690837">what</span> <span m="2691203">you're</span>
  <span m="2691568">providing</span> <span m="2691933">in</span> <span m="2692299">the</span>
  <span m="2692664">world.</span></p><p><span m="2693030">In</span> <span m="2693284">the</span>
  <span m="2693538">case</span> <span m="2693792">of</span> <span m="2694046">supervised</span>
  <span m="2694301">learning,</span> <span m="2694555">you're</span> <span m="2694809">providing</span>
  <span m="2695063">labels,</span> <span m="2695317">which</span> <span m="2695572">is</span>
  <span m="2695826">the</span> <span m="2696080">correct</span> <span m="2696334">label</span>
  <span m="2696589">associated</span> <span m="2696952">with</span> <span m="2697316">an</span>
  <span m="2697680">input</span> <span m="2698044">feature</span> <span m="2698408">or</span>
  <span m="2698771">with</span> <span m="2699135">an</span> <span m="2699499">input</span>
  <span m="2699863">data</span> <span m="2700227">set</span> <span m="2700590">or</span>
  <span m="2700954">data</span> <span m="2701318">point.</span> <span m="2701682">In</span>
  <span m="2702046">unsupervised</span> <span m="2702410">learning,</span> <span m="2702654">you</span>
  <span m="2702899">typically</span> <span m="2703144">have</span> <span m="2703388">no</span>
  <span m="2703633">labels,</span> <span m="2703878">but</span> <span m="2704122">also</span>
  <span m="2704367">are</span> <span m="2704612">limited</span> <span m="2704856">by</span>
  <span m="2705101">what</span> <span m="2705346">the</span> <span m="2705590">algorithm</span>
  <span m="2705835">itself</span> <span m="2706080">can</span> <span m="2706580">do.</span></p><p><span
  m="2707080">And</span> <span m="2707415">in</span> <span m="2707750">the</span>
  <span m="2708085">world</span> <span m="2708421">of</span> <span m="2708756">reinforcement</span>
  <span m="2709091">learning,</span> <span m="2709426">instead</span> <span m="2709762">of</span>
  <span m="2710097">a</span> <span m="2710432">label</span> <span m="2710767">per</span>
  <span m="2711103">data</span> <span m="2711438">point,</span> <span m="2711773">you're</span>
  <span m="2712109">providing</span> <span m="2712359">the</span> <span m="2712609">reward</span>
  <span m="2712859">information</span> <span m="2713109">to</span> <span m="2713359">the</span>
  <span m="2713609">system</span> <span m="2713859">that</span> <span m="2714109">says</span>
  <span m="2714359">if</span> <span m="2714609">you're</span> <span m="2714859">doing</span>
  <span m="2715109">more--</span> <span m="2715359">if</span> <span m="2715609">you're</span>
  <span m="2715859">doing</span> <span m="2716029">the</span> <span m="2716200">right</span>
  <span m="2716370">thing,</span> <span m="2716541">I'm</span> <span m="2716712">going</span>
  <span m="2716882">to</span> <span m="2717053">give</span> <span m="2717224">you</span>
  <span m="2717394">some</span> <span m="2717565">points.</span> <span m="2717736">If</span>
  <span m="2717906">you're</span> <span m="2718077">doing</span> <span m="2718248">the</span>
  <span m="2718418">wrong</span> <span m="2718589">thing,</span> <span m="2718760">I'm</span>
  <span m="2719097">going</span> <span m="2719434">to</span> <span m="2719771">take</span>
  <span m="2720108">away</span> <span m="2720445">some</span> <span m="2720782">points--</span>
  <span m="2721120">very</span> <span m="2721457">useful</span> <span m="2721794">in</span>
  <span m="2722131">very</span> <span m="2722468">complex</span> <span m="2722805">applications</span>
  <span m="2723142">where</span> <span m="2723480">you</span> <span m="2723874">can't</span>
  <span m="2724268">really</span> <span m="2724662">figure</span> <span m="2725056">out</span>
  <span m="2725450">the</span> <span m="2725845">labels</span> <span m="2726239">associated</span>
  <span m="2726633">with</span> <span m="2727027">each</span> <span m="2727421">data</span>
  <span m="2727815">point.</span></p><p><span m="2728210">Within</span> <span m="2728501">the</span>
  <span m="2728792">world</span> <span m="2729083">of</span> <span m="2729375">supervised</span>
  <span m="2729666">learning,</span> <span m="2729957">the</span> <span m="2730248">typical</span>
  <span m="2730540">tasks</span> <span m="2730831">that</span> <span m="2731122">people</span>
  <span m="2731413">have--</span> <span m="2731705">and</span> <span m="2731996">I</span>
  <span m="2732287">should</span> <span m="2732579">note</span> <span m="2732821">before</span>
  <span m="2733064">I</span> <span m="2733306">go</span> <span m="2733549">through</span>
  <span m="2733791">this.</span> <span m="2734034">There's</span> <span m="2734276">a</span>
  <span m="2734519">lot</span> <span m="2734762">of</span> <span m="2735004">overlap</span>
  <span m="2735247">between</span> <span m="2735489">all</span> <span m="2735732">of</span>
  <span m="2735974">these</span> <span m="2736217">different</span> <span m="2736460">pieces.</span>
  <span m="2736833">So</span> <span m="2737207">this</span> <span m="2737581">is</span>
  <span m="2737955">a</span> <span m="2738329">high-level</span> <span m="2738703">view.</span>
  <span m="2739077">But</span> <span m="2739451">we</span> <span m="2739825">can</span>
  <span m="2740199">certainly</span> <span m="2740573">argue</span> <span m="2740947">about</span>
  <span m="2741321">the</span> <span m="2741695">specific</span> <span m="2742069">positioning</span>
  <span m="2742609">of</span> <span m="2743149">everything.</span> <span m="2743689">I'm</span>
  <span m="2744229">sure</span> <span m="2744769">we</span> <span m="2745309">can.</span></p><p><span
  m="2745849">So</span> <span m="2746235">within</span> <span m="2746621">supervised</span>
  <span m="2747008">learning,</span> <span m="2747394">you</span> <span m="2747780">can</span>
  <span m="2748167">fall</span> <span m="2748553">into</span> <span m="2748939">classification</span>
  <span m="2749326">regression.</span> <span m="2749712">Unsupervised</span> <span

  <span m="2751429">clustering</span> <span m="2751872">dimensionality</span> <span
  m="2752316">reduction.</span> <span m="2752759">And</span> <span m="2753202">within</span>
  <span m="2753646">these,</span> <span m="2754089">there</span> <span m="2754533">are</span>
  <span m="2754976">different</span> <span m="2755420">algorithms</span> <span m="2755776">that</span>
  <span m="2756132">fall</span> <span m="2756488">into</span> <span m="2756844">place.</span>
  <span m="2757200">So</span> <span m="2757556">examples</span> <span m="2757912">could</span>
  <span m="2758268">be</span> <span m="2758624">things</span> <span m="2758980">like</span>
  <span m="2759336">neural</span> <span m="2759692">nets</span> <span m="2760048">that</span>
  <span m="2760404">cover</span> <span m="2760760">all</span> <span m="2761157">of</span>
  <span m="2761554">these</span> <span m="2761951">spaces.</span></p><p><span m="2762349">You</span>
  <span m="2763035">got--</span> <span m="2763722">just</span> <span m="2764409">take</span>
  <span m="2765095">regression,</span> <span m="2765782">PCA,</span> <span m="2766469">which</span>
  <span m="2767155">might</span> <span m="2767842">fall</span> <span m="2768529">into</span>
  <span m="2769215">dimensionality</span> <span m="2769902">reduction,</span> <span
  m="2770589">lots</span> <span m="2770901">and</span> <span m="2771213">lots</span>
  <span m="2771525">of</span> <span m="2771837">different</span> <span m="2772150">techniques</span>
  <span m="2772462">and</span> <span m="2772774">also</span> <span m="2773086">some</span>
  <span m="2773398">in</span> <span m="2773711">the</span> <span m="2774023">reinforcement</span>
  <span m="2774335">learning</span> <span m="2774647">world.</span></p><p><span m="2774960">And</span>
  <span m="2775292">there's</span> <span m="2775624">just</span> <span m="2775956">more</span>
  <span m="2776289">and</span> <span m="2776621">more</span> <span m="2776953">and</span>
  <span m="2777286">more.</span> <span m="2777618">If</span> <span m="2777950">you</span>
  <span m="2778282">open</span> <span m="2778615">up</span> <span m="2778947">a</span>
  <span m="2779279">survey</span> <span m="2779612">of</span> <span m="2779944">machine</span>
  <span m="2780276">learning,</span> <span m="2780609">it'll</span> <span m="2780986">give</span>
  <span m="2781364">you</span> <span m="2781741">even</span> <span m="2782119">more</span>
  <span m="2782496">than</span> <span m="2782874">all</span> <span m="2783252">of</span>
  <span m="2783629">these</span> <span m="2784007">techniques</span> <span m="2784384">over</span>
  <span m="2784762">here.</span></p><p><span m="2785140">And</span> <span m="2785380">the</span>
  <span m="2785621">thing</span> <span m="2785861">to</span> <span m="2786102">remember</span>
  <span m="2786343">when</span> <span m="2786583">you're</span> <span m="2786824">using</span>
  <span m="2787065">machine</span> <span m="2787305">learning</span> <span m="2787546">is</span>
  <span m="2787786">that</span> <span m="2788027">there</span> <span m="2788268">are</span>
  <span m="2788508">some</span> <span m="2788749">common</span> <span m="2788990">pitfalls</span>
  <span m="2789344">that</span> <span m="2789699">you</span> <span m="2790053">can</span>
  <span m="2790408">fall</span> <span m="2790763">into.</span> <span m="2791117">An</span>
  <span m="2791472">example</span> <span m="2791826">of</span> <span m="2792181">that</span>
  <span m="2792536">would</span> <span m="2792890">be</span> <span m="2793245">overfitting</span>
  <span m="2793599">versus</span> <span m="2793954">underfitting</span> <span m="2794309">where</span>
  <span m="2794582">you</span> <span m="2794856">come</span> <span m="2795130">up</span>
  <span m="2795404">with</span> <span m="2795678">this</span> <span m="2795951">awesome</span>
  <span m="2796225">model</span> <span m="2796499">that</span> <span m="2796773">does</span>
  <span m="2797047">really,</span> <span m="2797320">really</span> <span m="2797594">well</span>
  <span m="2797868">on</span> <span m="2798142">your</span> <span m="2798416">training</span>
  <span m="2798690">data.</span></p><p><span m="2799690">You</span> <span m="2800090">apply</span>
  <span m="2800491">it</span> <span m="2800891">to</span> <span m="2801292">your</span>

  <span m="2873621">data</span> <span m="2873988">or</span> <span m="2874355">what</span>
  <span m="2874722">we</span> <span m="2875089">call--</span> <span m="2875362">it</span>

  <span m="2882664">you</span> <span m="2882980">have</span> <span m="2883296">two</span>

  <span m="2889319">to</span> <span m="2889639">predict</span> <span m="2889959">a</span>

  <span m="2891239">So</span> <span m="2891559">if</span> <span m="2891879">we</span>

  <span m="2893299">the</span> <span m="2893760">diagram</span> <span m="2894220">on</span>
  <span m="2894681">the</span> <span m="2895142">right,</span> <span m="2895602">we</span>
  <span m="2896063">have</span> <span m="2896523">training</span> <span m="2896984">data</span>
  <span m="2897445">that</span> <span m="2897905">we</span> <span m="2898366">provide,</span>

  <span m="2901518">goes</span> <span m="2901907">into</span> <span m="2902296">a</span>

  <span m="2908232">a</span> <span m="2908527">good</span> <span m="2908821">job?</span>
  <span m="2909116">That</span> <span m="2909410">is</span> <span m="2909705">now</span>

  <span m="2911766">we</span> <span m="2912061">then</span> <span m="2912355">apply</span>
  <span m="2912650">new</span> <span m="2912999">data,</span> <span m="2913348">or</span>
  <span m="2913697">test</span> <span m="2914046">data,</span> <span m="2914396">or</span>
  <span m="2914745">unseen</span> <span m="2915094">data</span> <span m="2915443">and</span>
  <span m="2915792">look</span> <span m="2916142">at</span> <span m="2916491">the</span>
  <span m="2916840">predicted</span> <span m="2917189">labels.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2926598">here.</span> <span m="2926846">And</span> <span m="2927093">then</span>
  <span m="2927340">you</span> <span m="2927587">run</span> <span m="2927835">that.</span>
  <span m="2928082">And</span> <span m="2928329">you</span> <span m="2928576">can</span>
  <span m="2928823">see,</span> <span m="2929071">well,</span> <span m="2929318">is</span>
  <span m="2929565">it</span> <span m="2929812">working</span> <span m="2930060">well</span>
  <span m="2930936">or</span> <span m="2931813">not?</span></p><p><span m="2932690">And</span>
  <span m="2932951">most</span> <span m="2933213">of</span> <span m="2933475">these</span>
  <span m="2933736">algorithms</span> <span m="2933998">have</span> <span m="2934260">a</span>

  <span m="2936091">So</span> <span m="2936353">when</span> <span m="2936615">we</span>
  <span m="2936876">talk</span> <span m="2937138">about</span> <span m="2937400">machine</span>

  <span m="2938968">the</span> <span m="2939361">supervised</span> <span m="2939753">and</span>

  <span m="2941322">often</span> <span m="2941714">talk</span> <span m="2942106">about</span>
  <span m="2942499">training</span> <span m="2942884">the</span> <span m="2943269">model,</span>
  <span m="2943655">which</span> <span m="2944040">is</span> <span m="2944425">this</span>
  <span m="2944811">process,</span> <span m="2945196">and</span> <span m="2945581">then</span>
  <span m="2945967">inference,</span> <span m="2946352">which</span> <span m="2946737">is</span>
  <span m="2947123">the</span> <span m="2947508">second</span> <span m="2947893">step,</span>
  <span m="2948279">which</span> <span m="2948577">is</span> <span m="2948876">where</span>
  <span m="2949175">you</span> <span m="2949474">apply</span> <span m="2949773">unseen</span>
  <span m="2950072">data.</span> <span m="2950371">So</span> <span m="2950670">this</span>
  <span m="2950969">is</span> <span m="2951268">the</span> <span m="2951567">trained</span>
  <span m="2951866">model</span> <span m="2952165">in</span> <span m="2952464">deployment</span>
  <span m="2952763">or</span> <span m="2953062">in</span> <span m="2953361">the</span>
  <span m="2953660">field.</span> <span m="2954077">It's</span> <span m="2954494">performing</span>
  <span m="2954911">inference</span> <span m="2955328">at</span> <span m="2955745">that</span>
  <span m="2956162">point.</span></p><p><span m="2956579">Of</span> <span m="2957020">course,</span>
  <span m="2957462">no</span> <span m="2957904">class</span> <span m="2958346">these</span>
  <span m="2958788">days</span> <span m="2959230">on</span> <span m="2959672">machine</span>
  <span m="2960114">learning</span> <span m="2960556">and</span> <span m="2960998">AI</span>
  <span m="2961440">could</span> <span m="2961882">go</span> <span m="2962324">without</span>
  <span m="2962766">talking</span> <span m="2963208">about</span> <span m="2963650">neural</span>
  <span m="2964082">networks.</span> <span m="2964514">And</span> <span m="2964946">as</span>
  <span m="2965378">I</span> <span m="2965810">mentioned,</span> <span m="2966242">neural</span>
  <span m="2966674">networks</span> <span m="2967106">do</span> <span m="2967538">form</span>
  <span m="2967970">a</span> <span m="2968402">very</span> <span m="2968834">important</span>
  <span m="2969266">part</span> <span m="2969698">of</span> <span m="2970130">machine</span>
  <span m="2970366">learning.</span> <span m="2970603">And</span> <span m="2970840">they</span>
  <span m="2971076">certainly</span> <span m="2971313">are</span> <span m="2971550">an</span>
  <span m="2971786">algorithm</span> <span m="2972023">that</span> <span m="2972260">many</span>
  <span m="2972496">of</span> <span m="2972733">you,</span> <span m="2972970">I'm</span>
  <span m="2973206">sure,</span> <span m="2973443">are</span> <span m="2973680">familiar</span>
  <span m="2974046">with.</span> <span m="2974412">And</span> <span m="2974779">they</span>
  <span m="2975145">fall</span> <span m="2975512">well</span> <span m="2975878">within</span>
  <span m="2976245">the</span> <span m="2976611">supervised</span> <span m="2976977">and</span>
  <span m="2977344">unsupervised.</span> <span m="2977710">And</span> <span m="2978077">they've</span>
  <span m="2978443">been</span> <span m="2978810">used</span> <span m="2979165">for</span>
  <span m="2979520">so</span> <span m="2979876">many</span> <span m="2980231">different</span>
  <span m="2980587">applications</span> <span m="2980942">at</span> <span m="2981298">this</span>
  <span m="2981653">point.</span></p><p><span m="2982009">So</span> <span m="2982341">what's</span>
  <span m="2982673">a</span> <span m="2983005">neural</span> <span m="2983337">network?</span>
  <span m="2983669">A</span> <span m="2984001">computing</span> <span m="2984333">system</span>
  <span m="2984665">inspired</span> <span m="2984997">by</span> <span m="2985329">biological</span>
  <span m="2985661">networks.</span> <span m="2985993">And</span> <span m="2986325">the</span>
  <span m="2986657">system</span> <span m="2986990">essentially</span> <span m="2987398">learns</span>
  <span m="2987807">by</span> <span m="2988215">repetitive</span> <span m="2988624">training</span>
  <span m="2989032">to</span> <span m="2989441">do</span> <span m="2989850">tasks</span>
  <span m="2990258">based</span> <span m="2990667">on</span> <span m="2991075">examples.</span>
  <span m="2991484">Much</span> <span m="2991892">of</span> <span m="2992301">the</span>
  <span m="2992710">work</span> <span m="2992974">that</span> <span m="2993238">we've</span>
  <span m="2993502">seen</span> <span m="2993767">is</span> <span m="2994031">typically</span>
  <span m="2994295">it</span> <span m="2994560">being</span> <span m="2994824">applied</span>
  <span m="2995088">to</span> <span m="2995352">supervised</span> <span m="2995617">learning,</span>
  <span m="2995881">though</span> <span m="2996145">I'll</span> <span m="2996410">mention</span>
  <span m="2996702">some</span> <span m="2996995">that</span> <span m="2997288">we</span>
  <span m="2997581">are</span> <span m="2997873">doing,</span> <span m="2998166">some</span>
  <span m="2998459">research</span> <span m="2998752">and</span> <span m="2999045">actually</span>
  <span m="2999337">applying</span> <span m="2999630">it</span> <span m="2999923">for</span>
  <span m="3000216">unsupervised</span> <span m="3000509">learning</span> <span m="3001021">as</span>
  <span m="3001534">well.</span> <span m="3002047">And</span> <span m="3002560">they're</span>
  <span m="3003073">quite</span> <span m="3003586">powerful.</span></p><p><span m="3004099">The</span>
  <span m="3004473">components</span> <span m="3004847">of</span> <span m="3005221">a</span>
  <span m="3005596">neural</span> <span m="3005970">network</span> <span m="3006344">include</span>

  <span m="3854871">have</span> <span m="3855095">a</span> <span m="3855318">lot</span>
  <span m="3855542">more</span> <span m="3855766">detail</span> <span m="3855990">on</span>
  <span m="3856332">each</span> <span m="3856675">of</span> <span m="3857017">these</span>
  <span m="3857360">different</span> <span m="3857702">pieces.</span> <span m="3858045">All</span>
  <span m="3858387">right.</span></p><p><span m="3858730">Very</span> <span m="3858996">quickly,</span>
  <span m="3859262">we'll</span> <span m="3859528">talk</span> <span m="3859794">about</span>
  <span m="3860060">unsupervised</span> <span m="3860326">learning.</span> <span m="3860592">And</span>
  <span m="3860858">the</span> <span m="3861124">basic</span> <span m="3861390">idea</span>
  <span m="3861656">is</span> <span m="3861922">the</span> <span m="3862188">task</span>
  <span m="3862454">of</span> <span m="3862720">describing</span> <span m="3863098">a</span>
  <span m="3863477">hidden</span> <span m="3863855">structure</span> <span m="3864234">from</span>
  <span m="3864612">unlabeled</span> <span m="3864991">data.</span> <span m="3865369">So</span>
  <span m="3865748">in</span> <span m="3866126">contrast</span> <span m="3866505">to</span>
  <span m="3866883">supervised</span> <span m="3867262">learning,</span> <span m="3867641">we</span>
  <span m="3867887">are</span> <span m="3868133">not</span> <span m="3868379">providing</span>
  <span m="3868625">labels.</span> <span m="3868871">We're</span> <span m="3869117">just</span>
  <span m="3869363">giving</span> <span m="3869610">the</span> <span m="3869856">algorithm</span>
  <span m="3870102">a</span> <span m="3870348">data</span> <span m="3870594">set</span>
  <span m="3870840">and</span> <span m="3871086">saying,</span> <span m="3871332">tell</span>
  <span m="3871579">me</span> <span m="3871922">something</span> <span m="3872266">cool</span>
  <span m="3872610">that's</span> <span m="3872954">going</span> <span m="3873298">on</span>
  <span m="3873642">over</span> <span m="3873986">here.</span></p><p><span m="3874330">Now,</span>
  <span m="3874624">clearly,</span> <span m="3874918">you</span> <span m="3875213">can't</span>
  <span m="3875507">label</span> <span m="3875802">the</span> <span m="3876096">data</span>
  <span m="3876391">if</span> <span m="3876685">you</span> <span m="3876980">do</span>
  <span m="3877274">that.</span> <span m="3877568">But</span> <span m="3877863">what</span>
  <span m="3878157">you</span> <span m="3878452">can</span> <span m="3878746">do</span>
  <span m="3879041">is</span> <span m="3879335">maybe</span> <span m="3879630">look</span>
  <span m="3880055">for</span> <span m="3880481">clusters</span> <span m="3880906">or</span>
  <span m="3881332">look</span> <span m="3881758">for</span> <span m="3882183">dimensions</span>
  <span m="3882609">or</span> <span m="3883035">pieces</span> <span m="3883460">of</span>
  <span m="3883886">the</span> <span m="3884311">data</span> <span m="3884737">that</span>
  <span m="3885163">are</span> <span m="3885588">unimportant</span> <span m="3886014">or</span>
  <span m="3886440">extraneous.</span> <span m="3886813">So</span> <span m="3887187">if</span>
  <span m="3887561">we</span> <span m="3887935">observe</span> <span m="3888309">certain</span>
  <span m="3888683">features,</span> <span m="3889057">we</span> <span m="3889431">would</span>
  <span m="3889805">like</span> <span m="3890179">to</span> <span m="3890553">observe</span>
  <span m="3890927">the</span> <span m="3891301">patterns</span> <span m="3891675">amongst</span>
  <span m="3892049">these</span> <span m="3892699">features.</span></p><p><span m="3893349">And</span>
  <span m="3893657">the</span> <span m="3893965">typical</span> <span m="3894273">tasks</span>
  <span m="3894581">that</span> <span m="3894889">one</span> <span m="3895197">would</span>

  <span m="3900419">And</span> <span m="3900769">the</span> <span m="3901119">goal</span>
  <span m="3901469">is</span> <span m="3901819">to</span> <span m="3902169">discover</span>
  <span m="3902519">interesting</span> <span m="3902869">things</span> <span m="3903467">about</span>
  <span m="3904065">the</span> <span m="3904664">data</span> <span m="3905262">set,</span>

  <span m="3909450">cetera.</span></p><p><span m="3910049">In</span> <span m="3910324">unsupervised</span>
  <span m="3910599">learning--</span> <span m="3910874">one</span> <span m="3911149">of</span>
  <span m="3911424">the</span> <span m="3911699">difficulties</span> <span m="3911974">in</span>
  <span m="3912249">supervised</span> <span m="3912524">learning--</span> <span m="3912799">we</span>
  <span m="3913074">know,</span> <span m="3913349">right?</span> <span m="3913624">We</span>
  <span m="3913900">have</span> <span m="3914120">an</span> <span m="3914341">input.</span>
  <span m="3914561">We</span> <span m="3914782">have</span> <span m="3915002">a</span>
  <span m="3915223">label.</span> <span m="3915444">And</span> <span m="3915664">we're</span>
  <span m="3915885">like,</span> <span m="3916105">OK,</span> <span m="3916326">if</span>
  <span m="3916547">that</span> <span m="3916767">input--</span> <span m="3916988">if</span>
  <span m="3917208">my</span> <span m="3917429">algorithm</span> <span m="3917650">doesn't</span>

  <span m="3924259">my</span> <span m="3924782">performance</span> <span m="3925305">metric.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="3926782">there</span> <span m="3927100">is</span> <span m="3927418">no</span>
  <span m="3927736">simple</span> <span m="3928054">goal</span> <span m="3928371">such</span>

  <span m="3930526">the</span> <span m="3930773">algorithm.</span> <span m="3931020">Some</span>

  <span m="3932009">going</span> <span m="3932257">to</span> <span m="3932504">be</span>
  <span m="3932751">something</span> <span m="3932999">that</span> <span m="3933246">you</span>
  <span m="3933493">have</span> <span m="3933740">to</span> <span m="3933988">work</span>
  <span m="3934235">on,</span> <span m="3934482">is</span> <span m="3934730">at</span>

  <span m="3936978">I'm</span> <span m="3937300">most</span> <span m="3937621">having</span>
  <span m="3937942">that</span> <span m="3938263">separation.</span> <span m="3938585">Is</span>
  <span m="3938906">that</span> <span m="3939227">going</span> <span m="3939549">to</span>

  <span m="3940422">metric?</span> <span m="3940640">Is</span> <span m="3940858">it</span>
  <span m="3941077">the</span> <span m="3941295">number</span> <span m="3941513">of</span>

  <span m="3942386">creating?</span> <span m="3942605">Is</span> <span m="3942823">that</span>

  <span m="3945756">using?</span></p><p><span m="3946069">But</span> <span m="3946325">it</span>
  <span m="3946582">is</span> <span m="3946839">very</span> <span m="3947095">popular,</span>
  <span m="3947352">because</span> <span m="3947609">it</span> <span m="3947866">works</span>

  <span m="3948892">And</span> <span m="3949149">I'm</span> <span m="3949406">sure</span>

  <span m="3961540">of</span> <span m="3961840">networked</span> <span m="3962140">packets.</span>
  <span m="3962440">And</span> <span m="3962740">you're</span> <span m="3963040">trying</span>
  <span m="3963340">to</span> <span m="3963640">look</span> <span m="3963940">for</span>
  <span m="3964240">an</span> <span m="3964540">almost</span> <span m="3964840">behavior.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="3969400">is.</span> <span m="3969673">But</span> <span m="3969947">you</span>

  <span m="3977629">and</span> <span m="3977904">then</span> <span m="3978180">pass</span>
  <span m="3978386">that</span> <span m="3978593">on</span> <span m="3978800">to</span>
  <span m="3979007">a</span> <span m="3979214">supervised</span> <span m="3979421">learning</span>
  <span m="3979628">technique.</span> <span m="3979835">And</span> <span m="3980041">I'm</span>
  <span m="3980248">happy</span> <span m="3980455">to</span> <span m="3980662">share</span>
  <span m="3980869">some</span> <span m="3981076">research</span> <span m="3981283">that</span>
  <span m="3981490">we've</span> <span m="3981865">been</span> <span m="3982240">doing</span>
  <span m="3982615">on</span> <span m="3982990">that</span> <span m="3983365">front.</span></p><p><span
  m="3983740">Some</span> <span m="3984186">common</span> <span m="3984633">techniques</span>
  <span m="3985080">are</span> <span m="3985527">within</span> <span m="3985974">clustering</span>
  <span m="3986421">and</span> <span m="3986868">data</span> <span m="3987315">projection.</span>
  <span m="3987762">Clustering</span> <span m="3988209">is</span> <span m="3988656">the</span>
  <span m="3989103">basic</span> <span m="3989550">idea</span> <span m="3989768">that</span>
  <span m="3989987">we</span> <span m="3990206">want</span> <span m="3990425">to</span>
  <span m="3990643">group</span> <span m="3990862">objects</span> <span m="3991081">or</span>
  <span m="3991300">sets</span> <span m="3991518">of</span> <span m="3991737">features,</span>
  <span m="3991956">such</span> <span m="3992175">that</span> <span m="3992393">objects</span>
  <span m="3992612">in</span> <span m="3992831">the</span> <span m="3993050">same</span>
  <span m="3993269">cluster</span> <span m="3993547">are</span> <span m="3993826">more</span>
  <span m="3994105">similar</span> <span m="3994384">to</span> <span m="3994663">those</span>
  <span m="3994941">of</span> <span m="3995220">another</span> <span m="3995499">cluster.</span>
  <span m="3995778">And</span> <span m="3996057">what</span> <span m="3996335">you</span>
  <span m="3996614">typically</span> <span m="3996893">do</span> <span m="3997172">for</span>
  <span m="3997451">that</span> <span m="3997730">is</span> <span m="3998218">you</span>
  <span m="3998707">put</span> <span m="3999196">your</span> <span m="3999684">data</span>
  <span m="4000173">in</span> <span m="4000662">some</span> <span m="4001150">feature</span>
  <span m="4001639">space,</span> <span m="4002128">and</span> <span m="4002616">you</span>
  <span m="4003105">try</span> <span m="4003594">to</span> <span m="4004082">maximize</span>
  <span m="4004571">some</span> <span m="4005060">intracluster</span> <span m="4005549">measure,</span>
  <span m="4005845">which</span> <span m="4006142">is</span> <span m="4006439">basically</span>
  <span m="4006735">saying,</span> <span m="4007032">I</span> <span m="4007329">want</span>
  <span m="4007625">the</span> <span m="4007922">points</span> <span m="4008219">within</span>
  <span m="4008515">my</span> <span m="4008812">cluster</span> <span m="4009109">to</span>
  <span m="4009405">be</span> <span m="4009702">closer</span> <span m="4009999">than</span>
  <span m="4010333">anything</span> <span m="4010667">outside</span> <span m="4011001">of</span>
  <span m="4011336">my</span> <span m="4011670">cluster,</span> <span m="4012004">right?</span></p><p><span
  m="4012339">So</span> <span m="4012682">that's</span> <span m="4013025">a</span>
  <span m="4013368">metric.</span> <span m="4013711">And</span> <span m="4014054">you</span>
  <span m="4014398">iteratively</span> <span m="4014741">move</span> <span m="4015084">the</span>
  <span m="4015427">membership</span> <span m="4015770">from</span> <span m="4016114">each.</span>
  <span m="4016457">You</span> <span m="4016800">set</span> <span m="4017143">a</span>
  <span m="4017486">number</span> <span m="4017830">of</span> <span m="4018135">clusters,</span>
  <span m="4018441">saying,</span> <span m="4018746">I</span> <span m="4019052">need</span>
  <span m="4019358">five</span> <span m="4019663">clusters.</span> <span m="4019969">It'll</span>
  <span m="4020275">randomly</span> <span m="4020580">assign</span> <span m="4020886">things.</span>
  <span m="4021192">And</span> <span m="4021497">it'll</span> <span m="4021803">keep</span>
  <span m="4022109">adjusting</span> <span m="4022430">the</span> <span m="4022751">membership</span>
  <span m="4023073">of</span> <span m="4023394">a</span> <span m="4023716">particular</span>
  <span m="4024037">data</span> <span m="4024358">point</span> <span m="4024680">within</span>
  <span m="4025001">a</span> <span m="4025323">cluster,</span> <span m="4025644">based</span>
  <span m="4025965">on</span> <span m="4026287">a</span> <span m="4026608">metric</span>
  <span m="4026930">such</span> <span m="4027488">as</span> <span m="4028046">the</span>
  <span m="4028604">squared</span> <span m="4029162">error.</span></p><p><span m="4029720">So</span>
  <span m="4029947">in</span> <span m="4030174">this</span> <span m="4030401">example,</span>
  <span m="4030628">we</span> <span m="4030855">might</span> <span m="4031083">say</span>
  <span m="4031310">that,</span> <span m="4031537">OK,</span> <span m="4031764">these</span>
  <span m="4031991">are</span> <span m="4032218">three</span> <span m="4032446">clusters</span>
  <span m="4032673">that</span> <span m="4032900">I</span> <span m="4033127">get</span>
  <span m="4033354">out</span> <span m="4033581">of</span> <span m="4033809">it.</span>
  <span m="4034215">Dimensionality</span> <span m="4034621">reduction</span> <span
  m="4035028">is</span> <span m="4035434">the</span> <span m="4035841">idea</span>
  <span m="4036247">of</span> <span m="4036654">reducing</span> <span m="4037060">the</span>
  <span m="4037466">number</span> <span m="4037873">of</span> <span m="4038279">random</span>
  <span m="4038686">variables</span> <span m="4039092">under</span> <span m="4039499">consideration.</span>
  <span m="4039856">Very</span> <span m="4040214">often,</span> <span m="4040572">you'll</span>
  <span m="4040930">collect</span> <span m="4041287">a</span> <span m="4041645">data</span>
  <span m="4042003">set</span> <span m="4042361">that</span> <span m="4042718">has</span>
  <span m="4043076">hundreds</span> <span m="4043434">to</span> <span m="4043792">thousands</span>
  <span m="4044150">of</span> <span m="4044683">different</span> <span m="4045216">features.</span></p><p><span
  m="4045750">Maybe</span> <span m="4046054">some</span> <span m="4046358">of</span>
  <span m="4046662">these</span> <span m="4046966">features</span> <span m="4047271">are</span>
  <span m="4047575">not</span> <span m="4047879">that</span> <span m="4048183">important.</span>
  <span m="4048487">Maybe</span> <span m="4048792">they're</span> <span m="4049096">unchanging.</span>
  <span m="4049400">Or</span> <span m="4049704">even</span> <span m="4050009">if</span>
  <span m="4050338">they</span> <span m="4050668">are</span> <span m="4050997">changing,</span>
  <span m="4051327">it's</span> <span m="4051656">not</span> <span m="4051986">by</span>
  <span m="4052315">much.</span> <span m="4052645">And</span> <span m="4052974">so</span>
  <span m="4053304">maybe</span> <span m="4053633">you</span> <span m="4053963">want</span>
  <span m="4054292">to</span> <span m="4054622">remove</span> <span m="4054951">them</span>
  <span m="4055281">from</span> <span m="4055610">consideration.</span></p><p><span
  m="4055940">That's</span> <span m="4056309">when</span> <span m="4056678">you</span>
  <span m="4057047">use</span> <span m="4057417">a</span> <span m="4057786">technique</span>
  <span m="4058155">like</span> <span m="4058524">dimensionality</span> <span m="4058894">reduction.</span>
  <span m="4059263">And</span> <span m="4059632">this</span> <span m="4060001">is</span>
  <span m="4060371">really,</span> <span m="4060740">really</span> <span m="4061109">important</span>
  <span m="4061479">when</span> <span m="4061854">you're</span> <span m="4062229">doing</span>
  <span m="4062605">feature</span> <span m="4062980">selection</span> <span m="4063355">and</span>
  <span m="4063731">feature</span> <span m="4064106">extraction</span> <span m="4064481">in</span>
  <span m="4064857">your</span> <span m="4065232">real</span> <span m="4065607">data</span>
  <span m="4065983">sets.</span> <span m="4066358">And</span> <span m="4066733">you</span>
  <span m="4067109">might</span> <span m="4067414">also</span> <span m="4067720">use</span>
  <span m="4068026">it</span> <span m="4068332">for</span> <span m="4068638">other</span>
  <span m="4068944">techniques,</span> <span m="4069249">such</span> <span m="4069555">as</span>
  <span m="4069861">compression</span> <span m="4070167">or</span> <span m="4070473">visualization.</span></p><p><span
  m="4070779">So</span> <span m="4071086">if</span> <span m="4071393">you</span> <span
  m="4071700">want</span> <span m="4072007">to</span> <span m="4072314">show</span>
  <span m="4072621">things</span> <span m="4072928">on</span> <span m="4073235">Excel,</span>

  <span m="4074463">dimensional</span> <span m="4074770">object</span> <span m="4075077">may</span>
  <span m="4075384">be</span> <span m="4075691">difficult.</span></p><p><span m="4075999">You</span>
  <span m="4076352">might</span> <span m="4076706">try</span> <span m="4077060">to</span>

  <span m="4078476">to</span> <span m="4078830">the</span> <span m="4079184">two</span>
  <span m="4079537">or</span> <span m="4079891">three</span> <span m="4080245">dimensions</span>
  <span m="4080599">that</span> <span m="4080953">are</span> <span m="4081307">easiest</span>
  <span m="4081661">to</span> <span m="4082015">visualize.</span></p><p><span m="4082369">And</span>
  <span m="4082779">of</span> <span m="4083189">course,</span> <span m="4083599">you</span>
  <span m="4084009">can</span> <span m="4084419">use</span> <span m="4084829">neural</span>
  <span m="4085239">networks</span> <span m="4085649">for</span> <span m="4086059">unsupervised</span>
  <span m="4086469">learning</span> <span m="4086879">as</span> <span m="4087289">well.</span>
  <span m="4087699">Surprise,</span> <span m="4088109">surprise.</span></p><p><span
  m="4089339">So</span> <span m="4089570">as</span> <span m="4089802">much</span>
  <span m="4090034">as</span> <span m="4090265">a</span> <span m="4090497">lot</span>
  <span m="4090729">of</span> <span m="4090961">the</span> <span m="4091192">press</span>
  <span m="4091424">you've</span> <span m="4091656">seen</span> <span m="4091887">has</span>
  <span m="4092119">been</span> <span m="4092351">on</span> <span m="4092583">things</span>
  <span m="4092814">like</span> <span m="4093046">image</span> <span m="4093278">classification</span>
  <span m="4093510">using</span> <span m="4093790">nice</span> <span m="4094071">labeled</span>
  <span m="4094351">data</span> <span m="4094632">sets,</span> <span m="4094912">there's</span>
  <span m="4095193">a</span> <span m="4095473">lot</span> <span m="4095754">of</span>
  <span m="4096035">work</span> <span m="4096315">where</span> <span m="4096596">you</span>
  <span m="4096876">can</span> <span m="4097157">apply</span> <span m="4097437">it</span>
  <span m="4097718">in</span> <span m="4097998">an</span> <span m="4098279">unsupervised</span>
  <span m="4098560">case.</span> <span m="4098915">And</span> <span m="4099271">these</span>
  <span m="4099627">are</span> <span m="4099983">largely</span> <span m="4100339">used</span>
  <span m="4100695">to</span> <span m="4101051">find</span> <span m="4101407">better</span>
  <span m="4101763">representations</span> <span m="4102119">for</span> <span m="4102475">data,</span>
  <span m="4102831">such</span> <span m="4103187">as</span> <span m="4103543">clustering</span>
  <span m="4103899">and</span> <span m="4104243">dimensionality</span> <span m="4104588">reduction.</span>
  <span m="4104932">And</span> <span m="4105277">they're</span> <span m="4105621">really</span>
  <span m="4105966">powerful</span> <span m="4106310">because</span> <span m="4106655">of</span>
  <span m="4106999">their</span> <span m="4107344">non-linear</span> <span m="4107689">capabilities.</span></p><p><span
  m="4108689">So</span> <span m="4108978">one</span> <span m="4109268">example--</span>
  <span m="4109558">I</span> <span m="4109848">won't</span> <span m="4110138">spend</span>
  <span m="4110428">way</span> <span m="4110718">too</span> <span m="4111008">much</span>
  <span m="4111298">time</span> <span m="4111588">on</span> <span m="4111878">this--</span>
  <span m="4112168">is</span> <span m="4112458">an</span> <span m="4112748">autoencoder.</span>
  <span m="4113038">And</span> <span m="4113328">the</span> <span m="4113618">basic</span>
  <span m="4113910">idea</span> <span m="4114203">behind</span> <span m="4114495">an</span>
  <span m="4114788">autoencoder</span> <span m="4115080">is</span> <span m="4115373">you're</span>
  <span m="4115665">trying</span> <span m="4115958">to</span> <span m="4116250">find</span>
  <span m="4116543">some</span> <span m="4116835">compressed</span> <span m="4117128">representation</span>
  <span m="4117421">for</span> <span m="4117727">data.</span> <span m="4118033">And</span>
  <span m="4118339">the</span> <span m="4118645">way</span> <span m="4118951">we</span>
  <span m="4119257">do</span> <span m="4119563">this</span> <span m="4119869">is</span>
  <span m="4120175">by</span> <span m="4120481">changing</span> <span m="4120788">the</span>
  <span m="4121094">metric</span> <span m="4121400">that</span> <span m="4121706">we</span>
  <span m="4122012">use</span> <span m="4122318">to</span> <span m="4122624">say</span>
  <span m="4122930">that</span> <span m="4123236">the</span> <span m="4123542">system</span>
  <span m="4123849">has</span> <span m="4124210">done</span> <span m="4124572">a</span>
  <span m="4124934">good</span> <span m="4125296">job.</span></p><p><span m="4125658">And</span>
  <span m="4125883">the</span> <span m="4126108">metric</span> <span m="4126333">is</span>
  <span m="4126559">basically--</span> <span m="4126784">if</span> <span m="4127009">I</span>
  <span m="4127235">have</span> <span m="4127460">a</span> <span m="4127685">set</span>
  <span m="4127910">of</span> <span m="4128136">input</span> <span m="4128361">features</span>
  <span m="4128586">that</span> <span m="4128812">I'm</span> <span m="4129037">passing</span>
  <span m="4129262">in,</span> <span m="4129488">I</span> <span m="4129790">would</span>
  <span m="4130092">like</span> <span m="4130394">to</span> <span m="4130696">do</span>
  <span m="4130998">the</span> <span m="4131300">best</span> <span m="4131602">job</span>
  <span m="4131904">in</span> <span m="4132206">reconstructing</span> <span m="4132508">that</span>
  <span m="4132810">input</span> <span m="4133112">at</span> <span m="4133414">my</span>
  <span m="4133716">output.</span> <span m="4134018">And</span> <span m="4134320">what</span>
  <span m="4134622">I</span> <span m="4134924">do</span> <span m="4135226">is</span>
  <span m="4135529">I</span> <span m="4135878">squeeze</span> <span m="4136227">it</span>
  <span m="4136577">through</span> <span m="4136926">a</span> <span m="4137276">smaller</span>
  <span m="4137625">number</span> <span m="4137975">of</span> <span m="4138324">layers,</span>
  <span m="4138673">which</span> <span m="4139023">forms</span> <span m="4139372">this</span>
  <span m="4139722">compressed</span> <span m="4140071">representation</span> <span
  m="4140421">for</span> <span m="4140900">my</span> <span m="4141380">data</span>
  <span m="4141859">set.</span></p><p><span m="4142339">And</span> <span m="4142656">so</span>
  <span m="4142974">the</span> <span m="4143292">idea</span> <span m="4143610">here</span>
  <span m="4143928">is,</span> <span m="4144246">how</span> <span m="4144564">can</span>
  <span m="4144882">I</span> <span m="4145200">pass</span> <span m="4145518">my</span>

  <span m="4146790">narrow</span> <span m="4147108">waste</span> <span m="4147426">to</span>
  <span m="4147744">come</span> <span m="4148062">up</span> <span m="4148380">with</span>
  <span m="4148673">a</span> <span m="4148966">reconstructed</span> <span m="4149259">input</span>
  <span m="4149552">that's</span> <span m="4149845">very</span> <span m="4150138">similar</span>
  <span m="4150431">to</span> <span m="4150724">my</span> <span m="4151017">original</span>
  <span m="4151310">input?</span> <span m="4151603">And</span> <span m="4151896">so</span>
  <span m="4152189">my</span> <span m="4152482">metric</span> <span m="4152775">in</span>
  <span m="4153068">this</span> <span m="4153540">particular</span> <span m="4154012">case</span>
  <span m="4154484">is</span> <span m="4154956">essentially</span> <span m="4155429">the</span>
  <span m="4155901">difference</span> <span m="4156373">between</span> <span m="4156845">the</span>
  <span m="4157317">reconstructed</span> <span m="4157790">input</span> <span m="4158262">or</span>

  <span m="4161887">the</span> <span m="4162439">compressed</span> <span m="4162991">representation--</span>
  <span m="4163543">you</span> <span m="4164095">can</span> <span m="4164647">think</span>
  <span m="4165199">of</span> <span m="4165751">as</span> <span m="4166303">the</span>
  <span m="4166855">reduced</span> <span m="4167407">dimensionality</span> <span m="4167960">version</span>
  <span m="4168950">of</span> <span m="4169940">my</span> <span m="4170930">problem.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="4172979">some</span> <span m="4173333">work</span> <span m="4173686">on</span>

  <span m="4175099">are</span> <span m="4175452">also</span> <span m="4175805">really,</span>

  <span m="4178102">that</span> <span m="4178396">as</span> <span m="4178690">well.</span>
  <span m="4178985">And</span> <span m="4179279">finally,</span> <span m="4179574">we</span>
  <span m="4179868">have</span> <span m="4180162">to</span> <span m="4180457">talk</span>

  <span m="4183849">again,</span> <span m="4184329">at</span> <span m="4184809">a</span>
  <span m="4185289">very</span> <span m="4185769">high</span> <span m="4186249">level,</span>
  <span m="4186729">the</span> <span m="4187209">reason</span> <span m="4187689">reinforcement</span>

  <span m="4189410">different</span> <span m="4189791">than</span> <span m="4190172">supervised</span>
  <span m="4190553">or</span> <span m="4190934">unsupervised</span> <span m="4191314">learning</span>

  <span m="4192838">not</span> <span m="4193219">passing</span> <span m="4193700">in</span>
  <span m="4194181">a</span> <span m="4194662">label</span> <span m="4195143">associated</span>
  <span m="4195625">with</span> <span m="4196106">an</span> <span m="4196587">input</span>
  <span m="4197068">feature.</span></p><p><span m="4197550">So</span> <span m="4197831">there</span>
  <span m="4198112">is</span> <span m="4198393">no</span> <span m="4198674">supervisor</span>

  <span m="4217014">give</span> <span m="4217295">you</span> <span m="4217576">examples</span>
  <span m="4217856">of</span> <span m="4218137">where</span> <span m="4218418">reinforcement</span>
  <span m="4218698">learning</span> <span m="4218979">could</span> <span m="4219260">work</span>
  <span m="4219578">and</span> <span m="4219896">why</span> <span m="4220214">you</span>
  <span m="4220532">would</span> <span m="4220850">use</span> <span m="4221169">a</span>
  <span m="4221487">technique</span> <span m="4221805">like</span> <span m="4222123">reinforcement</span>
  <span m="4222441">learning.</span></p><p><span m="4222760">So</span> <span m="4223215">flying</span>
  <span m="4223671">stunt</span> <span m="4224127">maneuvers</span> <span m="4224583">in</span>
  <span m="4225039">a</span> <span m="4225495">helicopter.</span> <span m="4225951">So</span>

  <span m="4234714">whatever</span> <span m="4235007">you</span> <span m="4235301">just</span>
  <span m="4235594">did</span> <span m="4235888">to</span> <span m="4236181">do</span>
  <span m="4236475">that.</span> <span m="4236768">Could</span> <span m="4237062">you</span>
  <span m="4237355">create</span> <span m="4237649">a</span> <span m="4237942">supervised</span>

  <span m="4239590">doing</span> <span m="4240120">this?</span> <span m="4240650">Sure.</span>
  <span m="4241180">Right?</span></p><p><span m="4241710">You</span> <span m="4242042">would</span>
  <span m="4242375">basically</span> <span m="4242707">look</span> <span m="4243040">for</span>
  <span m="4243372">all</span> <span m="4243705">the</span> <span m="4244037">configurations</span>

  <span m="4248176">would</span> <span m="4248463">look</span> <span m="4248750">for</span>
  <span m="4249036">all</span> <span m="4249323">the</span> <span m="4249610">examples</span>
  <span m="4249896">where</span> <span m="4250183">your</span> <span m="4250470">helicopter</span>
  <span m="4250756">was</span> <span m="4251043">tipping</span> <span m="4251330">over</span>
  <span m="4251693">or</span> <span m="4252057">falling.</span> <span m="4252420">And</span>
  <span m="4252784">you</span> <span m="4253147">would</span> <span m="4253511">basically</span>
  <span m="4253874">say,</span> <span m="4254238">OK,</span> <span m="4254601">my</span>
  <span m="4254965">engine</span> <span m="4255328">speed</span> <span m="4255692">was</span>
  <span m="4256055">this</span> <span m="4256419">much.</span> <span m="4256782">My</span>
  <span m="4257146">rotor</span> <span m="4257510">speed</span> <span m="4257847">was</span>
